<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a> (1333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bombe</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:still.html>still</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bombe</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:early.html>Early</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:modern.html>Modern</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bomen.html>bomen</a> (2010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:transitive.html>transitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pole.html>pole</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:push.html>push</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:craft.html>craft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forward.html>forward</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pole.html>pole</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> shortening <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:older.html>older</a> phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opzetten.html>opzetten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:put.html>put</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:up.html>up</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tree.html>tree</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:same.html>same</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a>.
</p>
